# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccd77-102">.NET Framework 中的过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ccd77-103">本文中的表列出了 .NET Framework 4.5 和更高版本中由程序集组织的已过时的类型成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-104">使用以下链接可查看每个程序集中过时的成员和建议的备选项的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-105">本主题不会列出已过时类型的成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-106">有关过时类型的列表，请参阅 [过时类型](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccd77-140">系统程序集中的过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-141">下表列出了系统程序集中的过时成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-142">这些程序集用于面向 .NET Framework 的通用\-应用程序开发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="MicrosoftMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="ccd77-1139">Microsoft 程序集中的过时成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-1139">Obsolete Members in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-1140">下表列出了 Microsoft 程序集中的过时成员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-1140">The following tables list the obsolete members in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ccd77-1141">这些是特殊用途的程序集，包括面向单一语言（如 Microsoft.VisualBasic.dll）或生成系统（如 Microsoft.Build.Engine.dll）的程序集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ccd77-1141">These are special-purpose assemblies and include assemblies that target an individual language (such as Microsoft.VisualBasic.dll) or a build system (such as Microsoft.Build.Engine.dll).</span></span>
